## THE COMPANIES ACT

(Cap. 486 )

ISSUANCE OF CERTIFICATE OF INCORPORATION

PURSUANT to section 835 (1) of the Companies Act, it is notified for the information of the general public that the Companies whose details appear in the Schedule hereto, have been issued with Certificates of Incorporation.
